    <div class="about-text">

      <p class="section-label">Our Story</p>

      <h2 class="section-title">A Taste<br>of Home</h2>

      <p>At Suya Sundays, we bring authentic street-style suya to Atlanta and beyond. Every order is freshly grilled and seasoned with our signature spice blend — just like home.</p>

      <p>We focus on quality, flavor, and community. Whether you're an Atlanta local or ordering from across the country, we want every bite to feel like a Sunday back home.</p>

      <p class="about-tagline">"We focus on quality, flavor, and community."</p>

    </div>

  </div>

</section>
